The Passage of the Northeast Army into Tianjin 69

Cui Tingxian Efforts to Maintain Public Order

Jia, Xue and Jiang Arrive in Tianjin in the Same Car

Tianjin Correspondence: The details of the Northeast Army's entry into the pass to mediate by shortening the war and promoting peace through armed force were detailed in yesterday's letter. The army arrived at 8:30 AM today with three train cars, followed by a continuous stream of troops. Because there were still Jin army constables in the city, the Northeast Army did not disembark and enter the city. The details are described below. Tianjin Constable Commander and Garrison Commander Yuan Qingzeng was completely unaware of the Jin army's retreat and the Northeast Army's entry into the pass beforehand. Once it became a reality, he was extremely angry. As a result, he suddenly suffered from stomach pain on the 18th, and in the evening, he developed typhoid fever. He fainted once and was only slightly revived after emergency medical treatment. On the 19th, he also developed vomiting and diarrhea, and was unable to speak. His spirit was depressed, so Mayor Cui Tingxian had to bear the full responsibility for public security and troop withdrawal in the city. Cui, who has been in officialdom for a long time, can still remain calm in the face of major events. He arranged everything in an unhurried manner without revealing any panic. Public Security Bureau Chief Zeng Yanyi convened a meeting of the chiefs and officers of the five major districts and four rural districts at 8:00 AM yesterday (20th) to instruct them to fulfill their responsibilities to protect public order. At 11:00 AM, Mayor Cui also went to the Public Security Bureau to instruct the chiefs, officers, street chiefs, lane chiefs, and neighborhood chiefs in each district: (1) The Northeast Army's dispatch of troops this time is a peace movement, and it is benevolent. Local public order will still be maintained by the military, police, and constables as before, and there will be no accidents. (2) At this time of military urgency, it is inevitable that the reactionaries will try to take advantage of the situation and spread rumors. I hope everyone will remain calm and not be fooled. If there are bad elements who take the opportunity to cause trouble, they can be sent to the headquarters at any time for strict handling. Tianjin in the past is different from today's situation. Street chiefs and deputy street chiefs must also take responsibility to assist the police and constables in maintaining public order. (3) During this transition period, all organs of the municipal government and the constable headquarters have decided to continue to serve as usual. Before someone is officially sent to take over, they will never abandon their posts and leave first. In the past, when the situation changed, the new would come and the old would leave. This time, we have decided to maintain it to the end. Next, Bureau Chief Zeng's instructions briefly stated that he himself would be responsible for public security and would not retreat even if a knife was at his throat. The meeting adjourned at 12:00 PM and notices were posted everywhere prohibiting the spreading of rumors and disruption of finance. However, important figures in various organs who carried the Jin system color have moved to the various concessions since that day, their faces in a hurry as if a great disaster was about to happen. However, in order to encourage the serving spirit of the police and constables, Mayor Cui specially rewarded the constables with 10,000 yuan and the security team and police with a total of 7,000 yuan, and advanced the salaries for September of various municipal organs. The military organs also paid out the August rations, but they were Taiyuan banknotes. The previous night, the Jin army in Tangshan, in a hurry to withdraw and without cars to transport, beat the stationmaster. The railway bureau urgently telegraphed Shanhaiguan to ask Director Gao Jiyi for instructions. Gao replied by telegram ordering the rapid preparation of cars for transportation. The railway bureau then sent three trains. By 10:00 AM yesterday (20th), they had all been withdrawn. Xu Congzhou, the Chief of the General Affairs Office of the Beining Railway, called Director Gao to report to the chief of Shanhaiguan at 9:00 AM, reporting that the Jin army in Tangshan had left and requesting that Commander Yu quickly order the troops to advance. At the same time, a portion of the Jin army in Tanggu was also transported by the railway bureau in three trains by 4:40 PM. At 10:00 AM yesterday, the Northeast armored cars No. 1 and No. 2 advanced westward across the Luo River. Because the time was delayed by the station-by-station takeover, it was delayed until 3:30 PM. Three troop cars arrived at 4:00 PM. Also, at 2:00 PM, Yu Xuezhong and Gao Jiyi called Mayor Cui and Garrison Department Chief of Staff Zhu Xizhang in Shanhaiguan Public Security Bureau, saying that if personnel of various organs and garrison troops wanted to leave Tianjin, they could request cars from the railway bureau. Yu said that he had sent Lieutenant Colonel Chief of Staff Jiang Chunyan to Tianjin on the 102nd train to discuss the filling of the defense. Jia Jingde and Xue Dubi were also in the car, etc. At 8:00 PM, Cui Tingxian convened personnel of the organs at the municipal government to instruct everyone to serve with peace of mind and maintain it for a few days. Tomorrow is Sunday and they should work as usual. Wait until someone officially comes to take over before discharging responsibilities. At this time, they can handle the conclusion and prepare for the handover. After the handover, those who wish to return to Taiyuan should submit their names and the number of people to the railway bureau to prepare cars for transportation. At 8:30 PM, Director Xu received a call from Director Gao in Shanhaiguan, saying that if the personnel of various organs and the troops wanted to leave Tianjin, they should prepare cars for transportation at any time. All personal belongings should be allowed to be carried and should not be prevented. Xu asked Gao to come to Tianjin early. Gao replied that he was very busy coordinating military transportation in Shanhaiguan with Wang Fengrui, the head of the car affairs department, and that he could not come to Tianjin at this time because he was embarrassed by many things that were difficult to handle. It was decided to come to Tianjin with Yu Xuezhong on the 25th.

Yesterday afternoon, at 4:00 PM, the reporter interviewed Liu Encheng, the director of the Jinpu Railway Bureau. According to reports, the Jin army on the north bank of the Yellow River had completely withdrawn the day before. There were still more than 10,000 troops in Dezhou, who would completely withdraw on foot in about two days. The passenger cars of the railway had been requisitioned by the army, and there was only one locomotive left, which had been dragged into the Xigu factory and the parts were dismantled to prevent it from being dragged away by the army again. There are still five trains of troops between Dezhou and Cangzhou, which can all pass through Tianjin to Shijiazhuang tonight. It is said that Zhang Yinwu, the acting commander-in-chief of the Jinpu Railway, went to Shijiazhuang by car from Cangzhou yesterday. Feng Pengzhu, the commander of the 9th Army, is still in Dezhou.

Jia Jingde, Xue Dubi, and Jiang Chunyan arrived at Tianjin Station at 9:30 PM last night. Mayor Cui Tingxian, Garrison Department Chief of Staff Zhu Xizhang, Changlu Salt Transport Envoy Lu Jinli, Telegraph Bureau Director Bo Yizhong, Special Third District Director Wang Gupan, Public Security Bureau Chief Zeng Yanyi, and County Chief Shang De all came to the station to welcome them. Jia, Xue, and Jiang successively got out of the car. Xu introduced Jiang to Cui and Zeng, and after a few words of greeting, Jiang went to the Beining Railway Bureau to rest. Cui, etc., took Jia and Xue to the first-class waiting room for a confidential talk for forty minutes. At 10:30 PM, Jia and Xue left Tianjin for Ping. The reporter interviewed Jia and Xue, who said that the Jin army's retreat this time was ordered by Yan. The reporter also went to the Beining Railway Bureau to interview Chief of Staff Jiang. Jiang said that the Northeast Army would arrive at Tanggu and Lutai tonight, and would enter Tianjin in the morning tomorrow (21st). The armored cars would stop in Yangcun in the afternoon after departing from Tianjin. The army is filling the defense, and the area where the Jin army withdrew is the area where our army fills the defense, so the scope cannot be predetermined at the moment. Therefore, the takeover of the defense between Beiping, Tianjin, and Dezhou will be completed in a day or two. The order of mobilization of the troops for the takeover of the defense of Pingjin is as follows: 5th Brigade Commander Dong Yingbin, 6th Brigade Commander Li Zhentang, 2nd Brigade Commander Bai (certain), 27th Brigade Commander Liu Naichang, and 23rd Brigade Commander, originally Ma Tingfu, is now concurrently held by Yu Xuezhong. These five brigades all belong to Yu Xuezhong's 1st Army. After the 1st Army is dispatched, the defense of Shanhai Pass is replaced by He Zhuguo of the 3rd Brigade. Wang Shuchang's 2nd Army is also in the process of being dispatched and will soon arrive in Tianjin. Just now, I reported the progress of the negotiations to Commander Yu. My mission has come to an end, and I will return to Yuguan in a few days to report. (September 21st)

Inspection Report of the Luokou Battlefield 70

Jinan Correspondence: After the Jin army retreated from the north bank of the Yellow River at Luokou, I wished to understand the situation of the two armies' fierce battle across the river for forty days. This morning at 10:00 AM, I again followed a railway team's special train from Jinan to Luokou for inspection. The train arrived at Luokou Station after fifteen minutes. After getting off, I walked to the southern end of the railway bridge for a detailed inspection. Details are recorded as follows:

Battle Traces of the Two Armies: On the south bank, our army initially defended the Luokou area with the 61st Division of Jiang Guangnai's troops, followed by the 16th Army and 73rd Division of Li Yunheng's troops, and the troops of Zhou Qiduo. The construction of trenches and fortifications along the earthen embankment was extremely solid. There was also a fort at the southern end of the bridge. The houses where the bridge guards lived were destroyed by artillery fire. Bullet holes and marks from gunfire were visible everywhere in the nearby houses and trees. The villagers all dug underground to avoid the artillery fire. Now that the enemy troops have suddenly retreated, they are all extremely happy. On the north bank, the enemy troops were the 9th Army and 25th Division of Feng Pengzhu's troops, and the troops of Huang Guanghua. Their artillery positions were on Meihua Mountain behind Queshan at the northern end of the railway bridge. The mountain was relatively low, relying on Queshan as a shield. There were three battle trenches in total. The first trench was on the north bank of the river, stretching about five li east-west, curving in a wave-like pattern. Behind it was the second trench, and the third trench was along the Yellow River levee at the northern end of the railway bridge, forming three lines of defense. Between the trenches, there were communication trenches curving directly to the Jin army's headquarters in Beiluokou Village behind Queshan. There was also a fort in the center of the northern end of the bridge, facing our army's fort at the southern end, both protected by barbed wire and burlap sacks. Bloodstains were still visible in the trenches, and bullet holes were densely packed.

Damage to the Railway Bridge: The Yellow River Railway Bridge is a famous and massive engineering project in our country. On May 1, 1928, Zhang Zongchang's army destroyed one span when retreating north. It was repaired and reopened to traffic in June of last year. When the Central Army retreated to the south bank of the Yellow River on May 30 of this year, they could not bear to destroy it, and only dismantled one steel beam from the first span at the northern end (each span has ten beams) and seven beams from the tenth span (the largest span adjacent to the water). All the materials were transported to Pukou for preservation (one beam of material was not taken). The bridge body was intact, so when the Jin army arrived in Jinan, they only removed seven steel beams from the first span at the northern end and moved them to the span adjacent to the water at the southern end of the bridge. Because there was no water under the bridge at the northern end, they used wooden sleepers to support it, and traffic continued as usual for more than a month. When the Jin army retreated north on the 15th of last month, they used explosives to destroy the first wooden sleeper and steel beam at the northern end of the tenth span. As a result, the Jin army's supply train derailed at that point. The Jin army then poured kerosene on six of the beams supported by wooden sleepers at the first span at the northern end and set them on fire, turning ten thousand sleepers into ashes. The rails were warped by the fire, and the wooden beams also sagged slightly. The stones under the bridge were completely burned into lime. The intensity of the fire can be imagined. Bullet holes and marks from artillery fire were visible all over the bridge. The extent of the damage was unprecedented. The emergency solution now is to transport the original materials, add sleepers, and first install them to support the bridge for traffic. Wei Jinglu, the leader of the second railway team, his adjutant Li Yuhui, and Hu Shenghong, an engineer from the Jinpu Railway, are currently working day and night to supervise the emergency repairs. Fundamental repairs are currently out of the question. The derailed train on the bridge has now been pulled out. Once the materials arrive, it can be repaired and reopened to traffic within ten days.

Our Army's Pursuit: Sun Tongxuan, the commander of the 12th Army, led personnel from the army headquarters across the river from Luokou at 7:00 AM this morning to supervise the advance north. The first regiment of Zhao Xinde's 59th Brigade of the 20th Division has already crossed Yucheng. It is reported that the Zhaowang River Railway Bridge north of Yucheng was also blown up by the Jin army. As of today, the entire two brigades of the 12th Army, the first regiment of the pistol brigade of the General Headquarters led by Gu Liangmin, the 22nd Division of Cao Fulin's troops, the 85th and 87th Brigades of the 29th Division of the 14th Army, and the 64th Division of Ma Hongkui's troops led by Ma Tengjiao have all crossed the river. Cao Fulin, the commander of the 14th Army, will come to Jinan to replace Sun Tongxuan as the Jinan Garrison Commander. Cao's artillery regiment has already arrived in Jinan and is stationed at the Xinzhuang Barracks. (24th)

No Jin Troops Left on the North Bank of the Jinpu Line's Yellow River 71

Han Fuju's Troops Will Advance Toward Dezhou

Jinan Correspondence: Since the Northeast Army launched an offensive in Tianjin and Peiping, Feng Yuxiang and Yan Xishan have suffered major setbacks. The Jin army on the north bank of the Yellow River on the Jinpu Line, fearing their return route would be cut off, had no choice but to retreat north in a panic. At 7:00 PM on the 22nd, the Jin army retreated under the cover of heavy artillery fire from north of Luokou on foot. By 10:50 PM that night, there were no Jin troops in the vicinity of Luokou. At 6:00 AM on the 23rd, dozens of village chiefs and representatives of merchants from the Luokou north bank and Queshan areas came to the south bank of the Yellow River to welcome the Han army, requesting that they cross the river and advance north to maintain local security. The first regiment of Zhao Xinde's brigade of Sun Tongxuan's division of the Han army on the Luokou south bank crossed the river on civilian boats from both sides of the railway bridge at 6:20 AM, stationing one battalion each in Luokou, Zhao Village, and Queshan. The first battalion of Yu Huazhang's troops, who were the first to cross the river, were dispatched to advance north along the railway line. At 10:00 AM, Hu Shenghong, an engineer from the Jinpu Railway, and a railway engineer named Chen, traveled to Luokou on a railcar to survey the damage to the railway bridge. They returned to Jinan at 11:00 AM. At 1:30 PM, Dai Hongbin, the deputy commander of the armored train, also went to Luokou on a special train. At 3:30 PM, Fu Jianheng, the commander of the armored train, and Wei Jinglu of the Central Railway Team also took a railway team to Luokou for inspection. Both returned to Jinan that evening. At 3:00 PM, the pistol regiment of the First Army Corps arrived in Luokou on foot from Jinan and crossed the river and advanced north at 5:00 PM. It is reported that the vanguard of Zhao Xinde's troops had reached Yancheng at 4:00 PM that day (the 23rd) and are currently advancing toward Yucheng. The Jin army on the north bank of the Yellow River in Qingcheng retreated on the night of the 21st. Li Hanzhang's brigade of Cao Fulin's division of the First Army Corps crossed the river north from Qingcheng on the 22nd. On the morning of the 23rd, Wan Guozhen's 60th Brigade, Rong Guangxing's 87th Brigade, and Zhan Shutang's 58th Brigade also began crossing the river from Qingcheng, Qidong Taizi, and other places. It is reported that the two divisions of Qiao Lizhi and Zhao Mingyuan are also scheduled to cross the river in the next few days and will join forces in Dezhou within three to five days.

I followed Dai Hongbin, the deputy commander of the armored train, on a special train north to Luokou at 1:30 PM on the 23rd to investigate everything. After about fifteen minutes, we arrived. We inspected the Yellow River Railway Bridge. The bridge suffered considerable damage after the great battle. The wooden pile foundation of the first span at the northern end was completely burned. The wooden beam of the tenth span was bombed and broken. There were still several overturned and broken trains on the bridge. Many corpses and dead mules and horses had rotted and were emitting a foul odor. According to Yang Jinshan, an engineer from the Jinpu Railway in Luokou, the destruction of the railway bridge was all done by the Jin army when they retreated from Jinan to Hebei last time. There was no significant destruction during this retreat. As for the important materials such as steel beams on the bridge, they were transported south by the Central Army in June and are currently stored in Yanzhou. They can be transported here within a few days and can be repaired and reopened to traffic in about a week. (23rd)

The Fourth Route Army Recovers Liling and Liuyang 72

Changsha Correspondence: After the communist bandits' siege of Changsha failed, they fled in disorder toward Liling, Liuyang, and Pingjiang. He Jian, the commander-in-chief of the Fourth Route Army, immediately dispatched troops to pursue them on both the left and right wings. The progress of the past few days is described in detail as follows:

The Right Wing Army Recaptures Liling: The Right Wing Army consists of Li Jue's 19th Division and Chen Guangzhong's troops from the Xiangdong Bandit Suppression Command. They departed from the provincial capital on the 16th and pursued the bandits toward Liling along Datopu, Yijiawan, Zhuzhou, Banshanpu, Baiguanpu, and Yangsanshi, with Li's division acting as the vanguard and Chen's troops searching on both wings. Li's division pursued the bandits until reaching Baikaipu on the 20th without encountering any resistance along the way. On the morning of the 21st, Li's and Chen's troops divided into three routes and attacked Liling County. Most of the bandits had already fled to Youxian, Chaling, and along the old passes of Pingxiang, leaving only a small number of troops at Phoenix Mountain west of the city and the Yangsanshi Railway Station across the river to cover their retreat. They had not yet withdrawn and briefly engaged with the vanguard of Li's troops, including the detachments of Tao, Liu, and Wen, before fleeing toward Huangtuling and Youxian. The Fourth Route Army then recaptured Liling County at noon on the 21st. Li Jue and Chen Guangzhong entered the city on the 22nd. During the communist bandits' occupation of Liling for only one week, public institutions and the residences of He Jian, Liu Jianshu, Tao Guang, and others in their hometowns were burned to the ground. Communist bandits were widespread among the Xiangjiang military officers. The family members of all military officers with registered residences were kidnapped by the bandits, who extorted ransoms ranging from 1,500 to 20,000 yuan per person. The military officers were all in great distress upon hearing the news. According to reports, Zhu De, Huang Gonglue, Lin Biao, He Changgeng, and others fled to Youxian and Chaling, while Peng Dehuai fled to Pingxiang. There are two theories about the bandits fleeing to Youxian and Chaling: one is that they will flee to their old base in Jinggang Mountains in Jiangxi, and the other is that the bandits plan to invade Hengzhou via Caoshi. He Jian has ordered Li Jue and Chen Guangzhong's troops to pursue them from Liling toward Youxian and Chaling, while Ye Wenke and Guo Bugao's troops, along with the Liling militia, are pursuing them from Liling toward Pingxiang. He has also sent telegrams to the Gan army, requesting that they block the bandits in Pingxiang, Anyuan, Lianhua, and Yongxing, and to Commander Duan Heng in Hengzhou, ordering him to strengthen the defense.

The Left Wing Army Recaptures Liuyang: After the communist bandits' failure in Changsha, the troops of Li Shixing, Kong Hechong, Lai Ruchiao, and others fled back to their old base in Liuyang and Pingjiang. He Jian dispatched Luo Lin and Gong Bingfan's divisions to pursue them from Changsha, Longtoupu, Shuangxiqiao, Meiziwei, Leigongling, Fenglinshi, and Zhentoushi toward Liunang. Bai Shinuo, the head of the Liuyang Security Regiment, and Zhang Meicun, the commander of the Liuxi Farmers' Self-Defense Army, pursued them from Langlishi, Yongan Village, Jiaoxiling toward Liuxi. Zhu Xingshu, the commander of the Second Bandit Suppression Brigade, pursued them from Langlishi of Changsha via Jinjing to the north of Pingjiang. All of the above troops departed from the provincial capital on the 16th and have been advancing forward without encountering any resistance. Yesterday, He Jian told people that Bai Shinuo's troops had reached Wulidui near Liuyang City and would enter the city around the 23rd. The Liuyang County will be recaptured.

In addition, I would like to report on the statistics of weapons captured from the bandits. During the communist bandits' all-out attack on the province for half a month, there were two major battles. The first was from August 31st to September 4th, lasting five days and nights, and the second was from September 10th to 12th, lasting three days and nights. The bandits suffered more than 6,000 deaths and countless injuries. The numbers of casualties and captured weapons on the National Revolutionary Army side have already been reported by each unit and compiled by the Fourth Route Army Headquarters into a statistical table. A total of 473 of our troops were killed or injured. The numbers of weapons captured by each unit are as follows: (1) Luo Lin's division captured 2,007 rifles, over 500 spears, and 2 pistols. (2) Gong Bingfan's division captured 71 rifles, 39 spears, 9 hand grenades, and 5 bayonets. (3) Chen Guangzhong's brigade captured 740 rifles, 212 spears and flags, etc. (4) Li Jue's division captured 150 rifles and 1,083 spears. (5) Tao Guang's division captured 273 rifles and over 500 spears. (6) Wang Dongyuan's division captured 200 rifles, over 50 cattle, and 283 spears. (7) Peng Weiren's division captured 291 rifles and over 700 spears. (8) Brigade Commander Zhu Xingshu captured 38 rifles. A total of 3,870 rifles were captured. (September 23rd)

He Jian Shuts Down the Xiangxiang Minbao 73

Changsha Correspondence: After the events of July 27th in the provincial capital, the people of Hunan generally felt resentful and unable to vent their anger after suffering such a tragedy. The Changsha Citizen's Daily had previously published an article by Hu Yiru, the secretary-general of the Hunan Provincial Education Association, and others, requesting the central government to remove the Hunan party affairs authorities. Tan Changkai, the propaganda minister of the provincial party headquarters, immediately warned the newspaper with an order, accusing it of being close to reaction. The newspaper has remained silent since then. Unexpectedly, the Xiangxiang Minbao published an editorial short comment and an article in the party affairs column on September 17th that expressed dissatisfaction with the authorities. The key points of the wording were: (1) that the severity of the bandit disaster was due to the peacetime painting of peace and hiding of the sickness by Hunan's military and political leaders, leading to this situation; (2) criticizing the military authorities for guarding the Changsha fortress and not launching a quick attack, which was a bad plan; (3) that the Hunan Provincial Party Affairs Guidance Committee members all hold positions in Beijing and remotely supervise the Party Committee, receiving salaries but neglecting their duties, often unable to reach the legal quorum to hold a meeting once every few months, which was investigated and reported by the inspectors to the Fourth Route Army Headquarters. He Jian, believing that the newspaper was run by the Xiangxiang County Party Headquarters, ordered Wang Dongyuan, the Changsha Garrison Commander, to send 20 soldiers to Xiangxiang on the 20th to arrest Tang Weiliang, Yan Ying, Zeng Yu, and Tan Zuwu, the editors of the Minbao. In addition to shutting down the Minbao, he also sent Tang and the other three to the provincial military law office on the 21st for interrogation. The following is the text of He Jian's telegram regarding this matter: Telegram to the Central Government, Urgent, Nanjing Central Party Headquarters, Premier of the National Government, Tan Luhe, Commander-in-Chief Chiang's Hankou Headquarters, and Commander He Jian: I have been following the orders of the Commander-in-Chief and Director He to build fortresses and consolidate defenses in Changsha. The strategy of attack and defense is related to military secrets and has been reported at any time, but recently the communist bandits in the province have been seizing agencies and deliberately spreading rumors in an attempt to disrupt the hearing and hinder military action. If we do not strictly investigate, we will not be able to stop the chaos. According to the inspector's submission, the Xiangxiang Minbao of September 17th contained articles in the editorial short comment columns and the Xiangxiang County Executive Committee telegram in the party affairs column, fabricating military information, slandering the authorities, confusing the public, inciting chaos, weakening our morale, and increasing the banditry. The executive members of the party headquarters and the editors of the newspaper dared to be so unlawful, not only speaking out for the communist bandits but also plotting to cause chaos. I have informed the Provincial Guidance Committee and sent police to arrest them. He Jian kowtows.

Order to the Garrison Command: This army has been building fortresses to consolidate the provincial defense following the orders of Commander-in-Chief He. The strategy of attack and defense is related to military information, and outsiders must not speculate. Recently, the communist bandits have been seizing agencies and deliberately spreading rumors, so we must strictly investigate to stop the chaos. According to the submitted Xiangxiang Minbao of September 17th, the articles in the editorial short comment columns and the county executive committee telegram in the party affairs column fabricated military information, slandered the authorities, confused the public, incited chaos, and disturbed military morale. The executive members of the party headquarters and the editors of the newspaper are extremely unlawful. The Changsha Garrison Command is ordered to send officers and 20 armed soldiers to Xiangxiang to strictly arrest and escort the executive members of the party headquarters and the editors of the newspaper back to the province for investigation. In addition to reporting this to the Central Party Headquarters and informing the Provincial Guidance Committee, you must obey and not let them escape. (September 22nd)

Local Correspondence Songjiang 75

Photography Exhibition Scheduled: Since its establishment, the Songjiang Huating Photography Association has gone through three years of seasons and has held two exhibitions. I have learned that the association has decided to hold its third exhibition, which will be open to the public for three days starting on October 5th. Lei Weiting, a member who recently returned to China from Sweden, will also bring back many photos taken abroad to join the exhibition.

Shensi Steamboat Incident: The transportation from Sixing to Xinzhuang usually relies on the steamboats of the Litong Navigation Company, with three round trips every day connecting with the Shanghai-Hangzhou train, which is convenient for passengers. However, a medium-sized steamboat of the company caught fire at night while it was docked at the Sixing Zhongshi Bridge pier yesterday. Because there were flammable materials such as gasoline on board, the fire quickly spread and the entire boat was burned down, causing transportation disruptions for the past two days.

Suzhou 76

Appeal from Huizhou People in Zhejiang Who Were Burned and Killed by Bandits: The Suzhou Fellow Villagers Association recently received a letter from members Wang Zanxun and Jiang Zhiting stating that they had received a telegram from Huizhou merchants residing in Jinhua Wuyi stating that the bandit disaster in Wuyi County was spreading, and the people could not bear it. The town of Lutan in the county is only a few miles from the city and has long been a prosperous commercial center. Thousands of Huizhou people are engaged in business in the town. In the summer of this year, bandit leaders Shao Zemin, Xu Ziming, and others sneaked into the county's Dagong Mountain (which is eight miles from the town and has a dangerous terrain) and posted reactionary slogans and announcements claiming to be the Fifth Route General Commander of the Red Army Guerrilla. First, they coerced farmers to join the bandit party and resist the payment of rent. Then, they extorted money and forcibly plundered, and if they did not get their way, they would burn and kill. The shops were forced to drain their resources and were extorted for three or four thousand or five or six hundred yuan, etc. After several months of extortion, they hoped that they could rest once their wealth was exhausted. Unexpectedly, the bandits' greed was difficult to satisfy. On the afternoon of September 1st, they brought guns and equipment and came in formation, poured kerosene on the houses in Lutan, and set them on fire. The entire city was reduced to ruins, and the situation was no less tragic than in Changsha. It was an unprecedented disaster. The Huizhou people who live in Lutan are now destitute, struggling to survive, and have no way to appeal for help. They will soon fill the gullies. They tearfully ask you to forward their appeal to fellow villagers abroad to help them and to telegraph the Zhejiang Provincial Government to quickly send troops to Wuyi to thoroughly suppress the bandits and relieve their suffering. The telegram is urgent, and the tears are mixed with the ink. Therefore, we are reporting the situation to your association. We hope that you will consider the disaster suffered by the Huizhou merchants in the area and take immediate action to rescue them, and we pray that you will send telegrams to fellow villagers abroad to jointly urge the Zhejiang authorities to save them from danger. This is a matter of public concern.

Another Kidnapping Case in Zhouzhuang Township: The area of Zhujia Lake Jiangrenbang, where Zhouzhuang borders Qingpu County, has recently been occupied by gangsters from Pudong. Recently, the Zhejiang Provincial Defense Army and water police patrol ships have conducted raids and captured thirteen bandit boats. The defeated bandits fled before (the 25th to Zhou)

The three villagers of Zhuang Chenjiabang, Xu Lingeng, Xiuyilin, and Xiumei, were kidnapped, along with the three farmers' boats of Ye Tiuyun, Xiuyongfang, and Xiucheng. Price Increase for Telephone Service May Be Resolved: Zhao Chuanyu, the director of the Suzhou Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, received an order from the Ministry to increase the telephone rental by two yuan and immediately notified the General Chamber of Commerce to persuade businesses to comply. The General Chamber of Commerce repeatedly convened representatives of various industries to discuss the matter, but they all refused to allow the increase due to the current commercial difficulties. They repeatedly telegraphed the Ministry of Communications to request a postponement, but the Ministry did not approve. Therefore, the Chamber of Commerce convened representatives of various industries again yesterday (the 26th) to discuss the matter and invited Director Zhao to attend the meeting. As a result, the representatives of various industries initially only agreed to an increase of five jiao (50 cents), but the Chamber of Commerce agreed to provisionally add one yuan per month to be persuaded by the Chamber of Commerce. The Ministry of Communications, on the other hand, was petitioned by Director Zhao to explain the commercial difficulties.

Mine Union Cadre Acquitted and Released: Zhou Wenhua, a 33-year-old from Hangzhou, was the assistant cadre of the Mine Union in the Zaozhuang Mining Area of Yixian County, Shandong Province. On March 18th of this year, Zhou Shengfang and other workers in the Zaozhuang Mining Area reported to the Central Executive Committee, stating that the members of the Mine Union had reactionary behavior. The Central Committee sent officials together with the Yixian County Government to detain the four members of the union, Wang Dajing, Yan Yucheng, Zhou Wenhua, and Zhao Yike. They were sent to the Army Department of the Military and Political Department of the provincial capital. The Army Legal Department interrogated them, released Yan Yucheng and Zhao Yike on bail, and transferred Zhou Wenhua and Wang Dajing to the Jiangsu Higher Court on July 24th. Zhu Wenzhuo investigated the case, and Wang Dajing was found to have no suspicion and was released on bail. Zhou Wenhua was prosecuted and the case was defended in the criminal division, Yellow Bingdao presiding. The judge gave a verdict of innocence. Zhou Wenhua was released on bail yesterday. Zhenjiang Warden Zhao Fengxian was also entrusted with handling the case, but due to mismanagement, two prisoners escaped from Zhenjiang Local Court Prison in early this month. The High Court sent Judicial Committee Chen Ludan to investigate and return to the court with a report. President Lin issued an order yesterday to Zhao Warden due to careless working, he was given a major demerit and demoted to a prison guard, and ordered to switch places with Jiading Prison Guard Han Yuwen. Also, Taixing Prison Guard Xiao Yu was removed from his post due to an escaped prisoner, and the vacancy was filled by Cheng Zhunqi.

Major Fire at the New Suzhou Sericulture Farm: At around 8:00 PM on the night before (the 25th), a fire suddenly broke out in the first silkworm room drying tank at the New Suzhou Agricultural and Forestry Sericulture Farm in Nanyuan, Fengmen. The fire spread quickly and was extinguished at around 10:00 PM. After an investigation, it was found that more than 30 rooms had been burned down, and the loss of equipment, silkworm eggs, and property was about 70,000 yuan, which can be called a major disaster.

Du Jingwu Acting Captain of the 14th Team: Huai Zongbang, the captain of the 14th Team of the 3rd District of the Provincial Public Security Water Police Team, died of overwork. Wuxi 78

Three Thieves Arrested in Connection with Multiple Robberies; Public Security Causes Concern. In recent times, robberies have frequently occurred in Wuxi County and the surrounding four townships, causing considerable concern for public security. Magistrate Pan, recognizing the gravity of the situation, issued strict orders to his subordinates to intensify their efforts in apprehending the perpetrators. The other day, Wu Zhengrong, the police chief of the county government, received a tip from an informant stating that Yao A'yu, a wanted criminal involved in the robberies of Meng Bangjie and Xu Peixiu's families in Yantai and Tuntianli respectively, was hiding in Dali Villa, Hetou Shang, Area 51, Si Touzhen, Fifth District. Upon receiving the report, Police Chief Wu, along with over twenty officers, including Wang Wenzhong, Wen Ziming, and Zhu Liangji, immediately set out by boat at 12:00 AM. Arriving at their destination at 5:00 AM the next morning, they surrounded Yao Guozhang's house (Yao Guozhang is the head of Area 51 and Yao A'yu's brother). Yao A'yu, upon hearing of the impending arrest, hid in a woodpile. The officers knocked on the door, which was opened by Yao's wife. Police Chief Wu and the officers entered and searched the premises, eventually finding and arresting Yao A'yu in the woodpile. Several stolen items of clothing were recovered, along with deeds and other stolen goods unearthed near a large pine tree in Zhangcun Cemetery. All were escorted back to the city for interrogation. Yao confessed to participating in robberies in Yantai and Tuntianli and implicated his accomplices, Su Meigen, who was hiding in Zhou Shanbang, and Dai Hongda, who was hiding in Yantai Zhen. Based on this information, Police Chief Wu dispatched officers to apprehend the suspects. Su and Dai were subsequently arrested. A five-yuan banknote with a circular stamp belonging to Xu Peixiu's family was found on Su. It was reported that Dai Hongda was working as a teacher in a private school in Yantai Zhen. When the officers arrived to arrest him, Dai was loudly reciting aloud to the village children. Yesterday afternoon, Police Chief Wu escorted the three arrested robbers, Yao A'yu, Su Meigen, and Dai Hongda, along with the stolen goods, to the county government for legal proceedings and interrogation.

Lake Bandits Commit Robberies and Assaults. In Kaihua, Zou Huangni, Tianli, a resident named Wang Gancheng, a former member of the education committee, lived a modest life. Unexpectedly, around 12:00 AM the other night, dozens of lake bandits, armed with handguns, knives, and clubs, broke into his house and ordered everyone to be silent. Wang Ziqi and Bao were seized and forced to reveal the location of their silver. When Qi and Bao refused to speak, they were struck on the head, causing severe bleeding. The bandits then proceeded to ransack the house, stealing over 300 yuan in cash and clothing and other valuables worth approximately 200 yuan. After leaving, the bandits broke into the house of Wang Gancheng's uncle, Wang Xixian, and stole over 100 yuan in cash. Wang Xixian's daughter-in-law, Ms. Mou, had a pair of gold earrings forcibly removed, resulting in severe injuries to both ears. After the robbery, the lake bandits proceeded to Zheng Lanji's house next door and attempted to break in. At that moment, the security team from the nearby Wu clan, having received the information, arrived and fired shots as a warning. The bandits, realizing the situation, fled in a frenzy.

Investigation of Fish Farming. He Yushu, the Director of the Agricultural and Mining Department of Jiangsu Province, has designed various forms and instructions to compile statistics on fish farming in the province to implement fish farming guidance and fish fry transportation and distribution. In addition to instructing the counties to comply, he also instructed the county-run sericulture farm in this county the other day to investigate and report within three weeks of receiving the document.

Yao Ji Autumn Cocoon Firm Burglarized. Yuanfeng Silk Factory, located under the Beixin Bridge in Lihua Village outside the north gate of this county, leased the Yao Ji Cocoon Firm in Qianjia Lane, Chang'an Bridge, to purchase autumn cocoons. Since the opening of the weighing process, everything had been peaceful. Unexpectedly, the other day thieves dug a hole in the wall and crawled into the factory, stealing 2,400 silver dollars. Yesterday, the factory manager, Hua Budan, and the associate manager, Sun Junhe, reported the incident to the Public Security Bureau and requested an investigation.

Substandard Silkworm Seed Destroyed by Sericulture Suppression Office. Since its establishment this year, the Sericulture Suppression Office of the Department of Agriculture and Mines has worked intensely. From the spring silkworm season to the current autumn silkworm season, the office shut down 41 breeding farms during the spring season, issuing a total of 103 batches of permits with a total of 100 egg sheets. The breeding farms and the Japanese imported original and common varieties that were inspected by the Suppression Office and issued qualified certificates included 666,746 sheets of common spring and autumn varieties, 25,613 sheets of common summer and autumn varieties, 4,138 sheets of common spring varieties, 5,760 sheets of original varieties, 3,400 sheets of Japanese imported original varieties, and 200 sheets of common varieties. During inspections of privately made and transported and toxic silkworm eggs, there were as many as 20,419 sheets. With the approval of the Department of Agriculture and Mines, the office invited representatives from various agencies and organizations to gather at the public stadium yesterday and publicly burn the substandard silkworm seed.

Changzhou 79

The Arrest of Bandit Feng A'bao in Baizhang Town. Feng A'bao, a notorious bandit in Baizhang Town, Wujin County, possessed a box gun and was responsible for numerous crimes, including sending threatening letters, extortion, murder, and arson. Recently, the Baizhang Security Corps of the Fourth District learned that he was hiding in Wan Jiaxiang. On the 25th, at around 8:00 AM, they secretly apprehended him and escorted him to the Xiaoxinqiao District Office for a brief interrogation. Subsequently, the security corps escorted the suspect to the county government for further interrogation that evening.

Jiangyin Detectives Arrest Bandits in Changzhou. Li Dingzhi and Peng Genxi, two notorious bandits from Jiangyin County, fled to Changzhou due to strict pursuit in their own county. Huan Da, a detective from the Jiangyin County Public Security Bureau, discovered their whereabouts and secretly brought informants to Changzhou to apprehend them. On the 24th, at 10:00 AM, Peng Genxi was spotted outside the Great North Gate and apprehended with the help of nearby patrol officers. At around 9:00 PM, Li Dingzhi was spotted on Daguan Road in the city and also apprehended. Both were escorted to nearby police stations for custody. After Huan reported back to Cheng, Li Zonggang, the chief of the Jiangyin County Public Security Bureau, dispatched two additional detectives to Changzhou on the 25th to escort the suspects back to Cheng for interrogation.

Robbery and Assault During Arrest in Nanzhai Town. The other day, three bandits were gambling in a tea shop on An Yu Bridge near Nanzhai Town in the Eighth District of Wujin County. The water police stationed in the area secretly informed the Nanzhai Town Security Corps, who surrounded the tea shop at dawn on the 24th to arrest the gamblers. One bandit was captured on the spot, while the other two escaped. A gambler named Wang Heshang attempted to flee when he saw the water police arriving, and was shot by the water police. Jiangyin 80

Banditry in Dingtao Sandbar. He Qiren, a farmer in Dingtao Sandbar No. 2, received a threatening letter the other day demanding 300 yuan. The other night, more than twenty bandits fired eight shots and broke down the door, setting fire to his three-room thatched house and burning more than twenty dan of rice and dozens of chickens, ducks, pigs, and sheep. New Branch Directors Assume Office. Explanation of Alumni Association Organization. The County Party Rectification Committee requested the Provincial Party Department to interpret the organization of the Alumni Association of Changshou No. 1 School. The Provincial Party Department forwarded the request to the Central Training Department for interpretation. The instruction was received, stating that the purpose of the Alumni Association organization is to connect emotions and support the alma mater, which is in line with the spirit of the People's Groups Organization Plan, Section 3, which states that the group is for public welfare. The organization can be approved and belongs to a social group, and an application should be submitted to the competent authority for registration in accordance with Article 48 of the Civil Code. All methods, regulations, and content must meet the conditions stipulated in the Civil Code.

Prisoner Escapes from Detention Center. Due to the lack of housing and overcrowding in Jiangyin Prison, the number of undecided criminals has reached more than 400 in recent days. Yang Baoshan, an undecided criminal, cut the wooden edge of the railing with a knife and climbed onto the roof to escape. Zhang Xingzhong, a patrol officer from the Third Police Station across the street, spotted them during his patrol and apprehended the two criminals. Nantong 81

Li Changjiang Leads Troops to Yancheng and Funing to Suppress Bandits. Li Changjiang, the Third Commander of the Provincial Security Corps, is currently leading his troops from the Yu Shimei camps to Yancheng and Funing to suppress bandits. The Security Department has dispatched Xu Ying's Fourth Corps to Nantong to take over the defense. On the 25th, they arrived at Tianshenggang from Zhenjiang on the Hongda steamship. The camp headquarters has temporarily been set up at the Guangdong Guild Hall.

Joint Defense Implemented in the Northwest Fourth District. The towns of Pingchao, Tangzha, Liuqiao, Baipu, and Pi Lian in the northwest of Tongyi, as well as Rugao Zhentao, have suffered greatly from banditry. The county defense conference decided to implement joint defense in the four districts. On the 25th, a meeting was held in Liuqiao, which was attended by County Magistrate Zhang, Public Security Bureau Chief Zhang, and others.

Maintaining Charitable Institutions. The late gentleman Zhang Shen founded the Crippled Asylum, the Infant Nursery, the Old People's Home, and the School for the Blind and Deaf. Recently, Zhang Xiaoruo established a general management office. However, all the institutions are facing financial difficulties and are unable to maintain operations. All the directors have resigned. On the 25th, the board of directors decided to unanimously retain them and send representatives to Shanghai to discuss solutions with Zhang Xiaoruo.

Education Bureau Director Resigns. Song Binggong, director of the Education Bureau, has resigned. The provincial government has approved the resignation, and on the 25th, he handed over his duties to the newly appointed director, Guan Jincheng.

Zhenjiang 82

Dissolution of Mass Organizations in Various Counties of Jiangsu. Since the Central Government promulgated new organization laws for various people's organizations, all old people's organizations have lost their organizational basis. The Provincial Training Department has decided to plan to reorganize all people's organizations that do not conform to the new laws into legitimate people's organizations within two months. In addition to the provincial people's organizations, which were all dissolved three weeks ago, all people's organizations within the scope of the county will be dissolved within one month. The County Party Department will send personnel to take over and immediately carry out reorganization. However, the central government has not yet formulated regulations for the organization of farmers' organizations, so there is no way to follow them. Therefore, the county agricultural rectification committees and agricultural associations can only maintain the status quo temporarily. In addition, the industrial rectification committees in six counties, including Wuxi, Nantong, Wu County, Zhenjiang, Donghai, and Gangshan, are also temporarily suspended due to the large number of workers or complicated situations, and each association is responsible for directing the reorganization of various legal trade unions. During the maintenance period of farmers' organizations, the Provincial Training Department has formulated its work in accordance with local conditions. Generally, in areas where bandits and communists are rampant, the work of eradicating communists is carried out, and in areas where the local situation is stable, emphasis is placed on promoting the seven movements.

Yangzhou 83

The Chen and Zhang Children Were Kidnapped and Ransomed. On the 18th of last month, Chen Jintao's nine-year-old daughter, Xizhu, and the son of Zhang, a widow next door, Little Mouse, were kidnapped outside the Dongguan Aozi Street Mao Gu Lu Chen Firm in this city. The bandits repeatedly sent letters demanding a huge ransom. It was recently learned that Chen received another letter from the bandits, and the ransom price was slightly reduced. The meeting place was still in Zhenjiang. Chen entrusted Qi Xu to accompany Chen's eldest son and Zhang, the widow, to negotiate several times. As a result, the ransom price was 1,000 yuan. Chen prepared the money and went to redeem them the other day. The bandits collected the money and agreed to hand over the tickets at Quanlou, across the river. Chen and others went as agreed and waited for a long time but there was no sign of the bandits. Chen's wife cried loudly, thinking that she had lost her people and her money. While many people were watching, the two children were suddenly discovered on a small Yangzhou Zhen short-haul boat. Later, because the two children were crying on the boat, the steward was investigating the passengers carrying the children on the boat when he suddenly attracted the crying Chen's wife on the shore. Therefore, the mother and daughter and mother and son met in the crowd. The kind of ecstatic scene can be imagined. However, the two children were extremely thin, which shows that the life in the bandit's den is different from ordinary places.

Changxing 84

Wang Wumei Was Kidnapped and Escaped Danger. The other day, Lu Jiting, a resident of Changxing County, sent his relative Wang Wumei to lead workers to Yangmu Dou, near Yaojiaqiao, to collect rent. He was kidnapped by bandits, who sent a letter demanding a ransom of 150,000 yuan. It is now learned that Zeng Peiyu, the chief of the county's public security bureau, dispatched detectives to investigate in secret after receiving the report. It was learned that the bandits had hidden Wang Wumei in the Da Xiao Wu Mountains. He secretly dispatched a patrol team led by Tian, a squad leader, with three squads of armed soldiers and detectives. They rushed to the area at night and searched it carefully. When they arrived, it was midnight, and the bandits were trying to move the hostage Wang Wumei to Sian and then to Guangde. They encountered the bandits on the way and fought fiercely for a long time. The bandits were defeated and scattered in all directions. Wang Wumei was rescued from danger. However, it was late at night and the mountain road was rugged and the forest was dense, so it was not convenient to pursue them, so the bandits escaped and were not captured.

Jiashan 85

Taibao A'shu's Letter Leads to the Execution of Three Bandits by Firing Squad. After the Jiashu Bandit Suppression Command defeated the bandits in Fenhu Xidangtan and seized twelve bandit boats, the bandits fled to Xiaogang Ni'an in Luhu Nanhua. After a bandit suppression agent learned of this, he organized a team to go there, but the bandits fled again. The Ni'an was searched and a bandit named A'qi Jin was found. A letter from Taibao A'shu was seized, along with twelve nuns, old and young. The Ni'an was sealed. Later, a bandit named A'er was captured. A bandit named Hu Chong was also captured at the Dexin Building in Lu Xu Hedong. Hu confessed that Taibao A'shu had sent a letter asking him to buy 300 yuan worth of opium. Hu was sentenced to death and executed by firing squad outside Beizha on the morning of the 24th as a warning. A team was dispatched to search and suppress the bandits.

Ningbo 86

Change of Commissioner of Customs. The current Customs Commissioner Jiang, who is Japanese, has been handling customs affairs in China for 30 years. It is reported that Jiang has received an order from the Shanghai General Taxation Department that he will retire and be replaced by American Bode Li, a customs official from Harbin. He is expected to arrive in Yong at the end of this month to take office.

Huzhou 87

Two Mailmen Arrested by Security Team. At 5:30 PM yesterday, soldiers from the security team suddenly surrounded the Taihefang Post Office in this city. Several soldiers entered the office and tied up two mailmen, Wu Zhiliang and Wang Zhengfu. Onlookers were confused. It was later learned that a soldier went to the post office to buy five yuan worth of stamps. Because the receipt did not have the post office's insignia, the soldier returned to the post office to have it stamped. Because the person who originally sold the stamps was off duty, the person who took over did not know the details and said that he had to wait for the original seller to stamp it himself. The soldier argued with him for a while and then left. Not long after, the soldier returned with many people and arrested Wu and Wang. When the post office director saw that the mailmen had been arrested, he immediately called the county government. Because County Magistrate Li was out on official business, Secretary Tu Juyi called the corps on his behalf to inquire about the matter. Corps Commander Jiao replied that he did not know what had happened and would report back after investigating.

Xiaoshan 88

Fire at Fufeng Factory. The Fufeng Rice Mill machine room in Xiaoshan Ouwubang, outside the east gate, suddenly caught fire at midnight on the 20th. For a time, the flames soared into the sky and were impossible to approach. Fortunately, the volunteers worked hard to put out the fire. It is estimated that more than ten houses were burned, and the losses are incalculable. The nearby neighbors were also affected.

Taizhou 89

Wuyan Occupied by Communists. Yesterday (22nd) at 3:00 PM, more than a thousand bandits from Wenzhou suddenly came to Wuyan in the northwest township of Huangyan and carried out large-scale burning and looting. Xie Ren, the commander of the Fifth Corps of the Zhejiang Provincial Government Security Team stationed in Jiao (Haimen), urgently transferred troops and concentrated them in the city to be ready to advance and suppress the bandits. Linhai, which borders the county, and the county magistrate, Hou Changling, and the county party department urgently telegraphed the provincial government, begging to quickly send a large army to suppress the bandits to quell the chaos.

Replacement of Finance Bureau Chief. Zheng Zong, the director of the Finance Bureau of Linhai County, was dismissed from his position by order. Zhang Zhenfan was appointed to fill the vacancy.

Hangzhou 90

Communist Leaders Escorted from Ningbo to Province. The two Ningbo Communist criminals, Yu Rong and Zhang Qingxiang, were captured in Ningbo in the first month of last year. Zhang Qingxiang was sentenced to life imprisonment by the special criminal court, and Yu Rong was sentenced to nine years and ten months. They were escorted to the Second Prison. Now the Ningbo Municipal Government, by order of the province, has escorted the arrested Communists to the province for review by the military authorities. They were escorted from Ningbo to the province yesterday.

Chairman Zhang Returns to Province Today. Zhang Jingjiang, chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, went to Beijing to discuss the selection of the director of the Department of Civil Affairs and then went to the front with Chen Lifu, a member of the Central Committee, to meet with Commander-in-Chief Jiang. He has returned to the capital from the front and is scheduled to return to the province today (23rd). The issue of the director of the Department of Civil Affairs has also been resolved. According to the latest news, it is said that Chen Lifu, a member of the Central Committee, will be appointed.

The Science Department of Central University Will Go on Strike 91

｜Resolution Not to Issue Overdue Salaries Before October 4th

｜About to Implement and Demand Financial Independence

The Faculty and Staff Meeting of the Science Department of Central University was held at 3:00 PM on the 24th in the Science Building. Attendees included Cai Bao, Wu Shouchang, Zhu Jianren, Yuan Ji, Jin Shuzhang, Zhang Zhaoqian, Wu Suxuan, Shi Jiuzhuang, Zheng Xuedian, Ge Bowen, Zhou Xueou, Zhou Jiashu, Ni Shangda, Yang Xiao, Jiang Tianhe, Lu Zhi, Chen Yi, Fan Huiguo, Wang Baoren, Zhang Yizun, Pan Shu, Shen Wang, Li Xueqing, Wang Jiaji, Zheng Houhuai, Zhang Zhengping, Tang Kecheng, Chen Jieffu, Yuan Jianqi, Chen Guangqing, Guo Yicen, Li Niuzhong, Jiang Zhichao, Cao Yuanzi, Wu Gongxian, Zhang Zhenqian, Yu Jieshi, Zeng Zhaolun, Liu Shuqi, Ni Zeya, Chen Hao, Qu Mengzhou, Yu Xinzuo, Li Zhichang, Fang Guangqi, Xie Pengnian, Zou Song, Zhang Yu Zhe, Shen Qingnang, Zhong Xinhou, Duan Tiaoyuan, Zheng Lanhua, Zhang Jiangshu. The department heads jointly elected Cai Bao as the temporary chairman, and the meeting proceeded as usual.

The chairman reported that the department heads had discussed the financial problems of the department, and that salaries had been in arrears for three months. Although a declaration of salary demands had been issued, the end of September was approaching rapidly, and the school authorities still had no solutions. It was difficult for the department heads to maintain their positions; This is the first reason. 155,000 yuan of the school's expenses were used for general construction costs, 156,000 yuan was used for general office expenses, and 157,000 yuan was used for public expenses. Expenses such as experimental school tuition fees are not included, and the departments still have to pay for their own labor, stationery, and fuel costs, resulting in very little money being used for books, instruments, and experimental materials. The office equipment fee allocated to the department only accounts for 8%. This situation makes even the department heads tremble and fear. This is another reason why the department heads are silent. The aim is to convene a general meeting to discuss solutions. Now, in order to maintain the livelihood of colleagues, what attitude should be taken regarding overdue salaries? In order to improve the department fundamentally and properly, how should the funding be improved? Please express your opinions and discuss them together.

Resolution Cases (1) If the salaries for July and August cannot be paid before October 4, a department-wide strike will be launched on October 6. The proposal passed unanimously. (2) A declaration should be published in the name of all faculty and staff of the Department of Science. The proposal passed unanimously. (3) In order to improve the department fundamentally and properly, the school authorities should be required to fully fund it independently in accordance with the methods used by the medical and business departments. (The detailed implementation method will be discussed by the department heads) The proposal passed unanimously. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM.

All declared that salaries have been in arrears for three months. Even if we can serve the public on an empty stomach, there is no way to fund equipment and experiments. We hereby declare again that if the school authorities still cannot fulfill the requirements of the previous faculty and staff declaration before October 4 (next Saturday), we have to let it happen naturally, sit back and watch the shutdown, and not be responsible. We ask for your understanding of our meager grievances. Central University Department of Science Faculty and Staff Qi, September 24, 1999.

All Elementary and Secondary School Textbooks Must Be Submitted to the Ministry for Review 92

The Ministry of Education ordered the education halls and bureaus of all provinces and cities to order all bookstores to quickly submit all elementary and secondary school textbooks that have not yet been submitted for review to the ministry for review. The full text is as follows:

The Ministry previously found that many of the textbooks newly published by various bookstores have not been submitted to the Ministry for review, and has repeatedly ordered them to be submitted quickly. It is now found that there are still few bookstores that have not complied with the order to submit the various textbooks newly issued between bookstores, and there are even more high school textbooks that have not been submitted for review. Such repeated delays are completely inappropriate. In addition to issuing separate orders, it is also ordered that the provincial bookstores quickly submit all elementary and secondary school textbooks that have not yet been submitted for review to the Ministry for review, and must not delay any further. This order.

All staff of the office are assigned by the Ministry in accordance with the revised organization outline of the Overseas Student Supervision Office in Japan. You should know this.

Changes to the Far Eastern Games Competition Rules

The Chinese Sports Association is About to Publish New Rules 110

The rules for the sports competitions of the Far Eastern Games have been discussed and revised by the representatives of various countries at the meeting held in Tokyo during the 9th Games. After the closing of the conference, the draft program was prepared by the Japan Amateur Sports Association and submitted to China and the Philippines for review so that it can be implemented in the next Games. The procedure has now been completed, and the China National Sports Association is engaged in revising and translating the new rules (track and field and volleyball) for domestic adoption. Excerpts are as follows:

(1) Track and field and all-around sports adopt the rules established by the World Games, with many changes compared to the old rules.

(2) Volleyball has been re-edited by the Far Eastern Sports Association, with changes compared to the old rules.

(3) Football adopts the rules of the World Amateur Football Association, which are the same as the original ones, with only slight revisions. (1) Each match can have two substitutes (2) Players who are disqualified from the match cannot be substituted (3) Substitutes should enter the field during a dead ball, and the referee must be notified before entering the field.

(4) Swimming adopts the rules of the World Swimming Association, which are the same as the old ones.

(5) Baseball adopts the rules printed in the (SpoidngsBascballGuide) book, which are the same as the old ones.

(6) Basketball uses the rules set by the American Joint Basketball Rules (onmitlee), which are the same as the original ones and the ones used domestically.

(7) Lawn tennis uses the World Davis Cup system for grass courts, but there are no challenge week matches.

(8) Women's sports competitions in the Far Eastern Games are all for demonstration purposes and have no championships.

(9) The Japanese Amateur Sports Association proposed this spring to change the women's basketball rules to the men's basketball rules, but because China and the Philippines objected, the original proposal has been cancelled, so the women's rules are still in effect.

The track and field, all-around sports, and volleyball rules have been revised and printed by the National Sports Association and will be published in about two weeks.

Wang Zhengting and Wang Jiazhen Arrived in Shanghai Together Last Night 121

Wang and Xu Depart North This Morning to Receive Weihaiwei. Negotiations on British and French Rights Scheduled to Resume at the End of October. Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting, accompanied by Deputy Foreign Minister Wang Jiazhen, arrived in Shanghai by train from Beijing at 10:15 last night. Our newspaper reporter specially visited and interviewed them. The conversations of the two gentlemen are recorded as follows: Wang Jiazhen Discusses. The reporter inquired about the Weihaiwei takeover, etc. According to Wang, the takeover ceremony of Weihaiwei is scheduled to be held in Weihaiwei on October 1. Except for Liugong Island, all properties in Weihaiwei will be taken over. As for customs and postal services, the General Administration of Customs and the Post Office will directly send personnel to take over management. I am only going to Weihaiwei to attend the handover ceremony as a representative of our country. After that, Commissioner Xu Zushen will be responsible for the administrative management. I will stay in Weihaiwei for about ten days and then return to Beijing to take care of matters. Traveling by Warship. Wang also said that Mr. Xu Zushen has important matters and took a plane to Shanghai this afternoon (yesterday). I, together with Mr. Xu and handover personnel Zhu Shiquan and Kuang Guanglin, are scheduled to take the Fengtian Maru to Qingdao first thing tomorrow morning (this morning), and then take a warship to Weihaiwei. The remaining handover personnel, Ge Zuguang, Lao Weixiu, and Fang Zuchong, will take the Shuntian Lun to Weihaiwei on the same day.

Wang Zhengting Talks. Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting told our reporter that the results of the negotiations with the British envoy have been signed and resolved in three areas: (1) the takeover of Weihaiwei; (2) the distribution of the British Boxer Indemnity; and (3) the recovery of the Xiamen British Concession. The scope of the Xiamen British Concession is quite small. This signature resolution recognizes the abandonment of management rights by the other party, and our country's recovery has officially come to an end without the need for any further recovery procedures. Regarding the British extraterritorial rights, the British side has now put forward a new opinion, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is studying and considering it and has not yet replied to the British envoy. After staying in Shanghai for a few days, he will return to Beiping and has agreed with me to go south at the end of October to continue negotiations on extraterritorial rights. Also, French envoy Weirton is scheduled to go south on October 16 to discuss the recovery of the French Concession. At that time, if President Jiang has returned to Beijing, the letter of credence will be presented in person.

Mayor Zhang Sends a Telegram to Resign as Chairman of the China Merchants Bureau Reorganization Committee 122

The State Council has decided to appoint Mayor Zhang and seven others as members of the China Merchants Bureau Reorganization Committee, and designated Mayor Zhang as the chairman. Mayor Zhang, who was on official business in Liaoning, learned of this news and felt that the China Merchants Bureau is related to the national shipping industry and urgently needs a thorough reorganization. He himself is the mayor and has heavy responsibilities. It is inconvenient to concurrently serve as the chairman of the China Merchants Bureau Reorganization Committee. Therefore, he telegraphed the central government to resign sincerely. The original telegram is recorded as follows: Urgent to the Nanjing National Government, I, Zhang Qun, was recently informed by the Shanghai News that your government has decided to appoint me as the chairman of the China Merchants Bureau Reorganization Committee. I am deeply disturbed by this news. When I first took up the post of mayor, I resigned from all the other positions I held, intending that a person with no talent can concentrate on one thing, and I am worried that I will be exhausted by one position, let alone others. In recent years, I have been running north and south for national affairs, and I have asked myself that there are still many shortcomings in the matters of Shanghai's prosperity and reform. Concurrently managing other things will only make things worse. Moreover, the reorganization of the bureau requires specialized knowledge and experience. What's more, your government is eagerly seeking governance, and there are still many talented people who have been wasted and not restored. At this time of comprehensive renewal of the political system, it is the time to employ talents without any restrictions. As the China Merchants Bureau is related to the national shipping industry, it should be widely visited by talents and thoroughly reorganized. My own presence in the council is not suitable for this. I humbly resign and hope that you will understand, Zhang Qun respectfully bows.
